						limit = { any_core_state = { internet_station < 1 } }
						random_core_state = {
							limit = { internet_station < 1 }
							add_building_construction = {
								type = internet_station
								level = 1
								instant_build = yes
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { PER_internet_station_cost = -3 }
						}

				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = PER_internet_station_cost }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = PER_internet_coverage_effect_TT

					add_building_construction = {

					}

				}
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [THIS.GetName]: Focus PER_guided_by_people"
			set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 10 }
			change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
			newline = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_guardian_council_block_TT
			# If this focus is taken before 2001 Elections, Ebrahim Yazdi Replaces Khatami
			if = {
				limit = {
					date < 2001.2.1
				}
				set_country_flag = PER_yazdi_goes
			}
			# If Focus taken right before 2005 Elections, Mostafa Kavakebian replaces Rafsanjani
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date < 2005.2.1
				}
				set_country_flag = PER_kavakebian_goes
			}
			# If Focus taken right before 2009, Mehdi Karroubi Replaces Mousavi
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date > 2009.2.1
				}
				set_country_flag = PER_karroubi_goes
			}
			# If Focus taken right before 2013, Mashaei Replaces Ahmadinejad
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date > 2013.2.1
				}
				set_country_flag = PER_mashaei_goes
			}
			# If focus taken right before 2017, Hassan Bayadi replaces Raisi
